101 def getPrefixAndLen(item):
102  ip = netaddr.IPNetwork(item)
103  return (ip.value, ip.prefixlen)
104 
105 def getPrefix(item):
106  ip = netaddr.IPNetwork(item['prefix'])
107  return int(ip.ip)
108 
109 def getNbr(item):
110  ip = netaddr.IPNetwork(item['neighbor-address'])
111  return int(ip.ip)
112 
113 def getIntfId(item):
114 
115  ifName = item['neighbor-address']
116  if ifName.startswith("Ethernet"):
117  nums = ifName[len("Ethernet"):].split('.')
118  ifId = int(nums[0]) * 2 ** 32
119  if len(nums) > 1:
120  ifId += int(nums[1])
121  elif ifName.startswith("PortChannel"):
122  nums = ifName[len("PortChannel"):].split('.')
123  ifId = int(nums[0]) * 2 ** 32
124  if len(nums) > 1:
125  ifId += int(nums[1])
126  elif ifName.startswith("Vlan"):
127  ifId = int(ifName[len("Vlan"):])
128  elif ifName.startswith("Loopback"):
129  ifId = int(ifName[len("Loopback"):])
130  else:
131  return ifName
132  return ifId

135 def generate_show_bgp_routes(args):
136  api = cc.ApiClient()
137  keypath = []
138  body = None
139  afisafi = "IPV4_UNICAST"
140  rib_type = "ipv4-unicast"
141  vrf = "default"
142  neighbour_ip = ''
143  route_option = 'loc-rib'
144  querytype = None
145  rfilter = None
146  i = 0
147  for arg in args:
148  if "vrf" == arg:
149  vrf = args[i+1]
150  elif "ipv4" == arg:
151  afisafi = "IPV4_UNICAST"
152  rib_type = "ipv4-unicast"
153  elif "ipv6" == arg:
154  afisafi = "IPV6_UNICAST"
155  rib_type = "ipv6-unicast"
156  elif "neighbors" == arg:
157  ni = i+2 if "interface" == args[i+1] else i+1
158  neighbour_ip = args[ni]
159  route_option = args[ni+1]
160  elif "ip-addr" == arg:
161  querytype = 'IP-ADDR'
162  elif "community" == arg:
163  querytype = 'COMMUNITY-STRING'
164  aann = args[i+1]
165  elif "local-as" == arg:
166  querytype = 'COMMUNITY-LOCAL-AS'
167  elif "no-advertise" == arg:
168  querytype = 'COMMUNITY-NO-ADVERTISE'
169  elif "no-export" == arg:
170  querytype = 'COMMUNITY-NO-EXPORT'
171  elif "no-peer" == arg:
172  querytype = 'COMMUNITY-NO-PEER'
173  elif "bestpath" == arg:
174  rfilter = 'BEST_PATH'
175  elif "multipath" == arg:
176  rfilter = 'MULTI_PATH'
177  elif "exact-match" == arg:
178  rfilter = arg
179  elif "route-map" == arg:
180  querytype = 'ROUTE-MAP'
181  rtmapname = args[i+1]
182  else:
183  if querytype == 'IP-ADDR':
184  ipstr = arg
185  else:
186  pass
187  i = i + 1
188  d = {}
189  method = "rpc"
190  if route_option == "loc-rib":
191  if method == 'rpc':
192  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/operations/sonic-bgp-show:show-bgp')
193  inputs = {"vrf-name":vrf, "address-family":afisafi}
194  if querytype:
195  inputs['query-type'] = querytype
196  if querytype == 'IP-ADDR':
197  inputs['ip-addr'] = ipstr
198  if rfilter:
199  inputs['path-type'] = rfilter
200  elif querytype == 'COMMUNITY-STRING':
201  inputs['community-string'] = aann
202  if "exact-match" == rfilter:
203  inputs['community-str-exact-match'] = True
204  elif querytype == 'COMMUNITY-LOCAL-AS':
205  if "exact-match" == rfilter:
206  inputs['community-local-as-exact-match'] = True
207  elif querytype == 'COMMUNITY-NO-ADVERTISE':
208  if "exact-match" == rfilter:
209  inputs['community-no-advertise-exact-match'] = True
210  elif querytype == 'COMMUNITY-NO-EXPORT':
211  if "exact-match" == rfilter:
212  inputs['community-no-export-exact-match'] = True
213  elif querytype == 'COMMUNITY-NO-PEER':
214  if "exact-match" == rfilter:
215  inputs['community-no-peer-exact-match'] = True
216  elif querytype == 'ROUTE-MAP':
217  inputs['route-map-name'] = rtmapname
218  body = {"sonic-bgp-show:input": inputs}
219  response = api.post(keypath, body)
220  if not response:
221  # unknown error (bad input?)
222  return 1
223  if(response.ok()):
224  d = response.content['sonic-bgp-show:output']['response']
225  if len(d) != 0 and "warning" not in d and "Unknown command:" not in d:
226  try:
227  d = json.loads(d)
228  except:
229  # unknown or missing output
230  return 1
231  if querytype == 'IP-ADDR':
232  prf = d.get("prefix")
233  if not prf:
234  # no routes
235  return 0
236  show_cli_output("show_bgp_ipaddr_routes_rpc.j2", d)
237  else:
238  routes = d.get("routes")
239  if not routes:
240  # no routes
241  return 0
242  keys = sorted(routes,key=getPrefixAndLen)
243  temp = OrderedDict()
244  for key in keys:
245  temp[key] = routes[key]
246 
247  d["routes"] = temp
248 
249  show_cli_output("show_ip_bgp_routes_rpc.j2", d)
250  else:
251  print response.error_message()
252  return 1
253 
254  else:
255  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/global', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER,name1=NAME1)
256  response = api.get(keypath)
257  if(response.ok() and response.content is not None):
258  d.update(response.content)
259  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/rib/afi-safis/afi-safi={afi_safi_name}/{type_name}/loc-rib', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER, name1=NAME1, afi_safi_name=afisafi, type_name=rib_type)
260  response1 = api.get(keypath)
261  if(response1.ok() and response1.content is not None):
262  if 'openconfig-network-instance:loc-rib' in response1.content:
263  route = response1.content['openconfig-network-instance:loc-rib']['routes']
264  tup = route['route']
265  route['route'] = sorted(tup, key=getPrefix)
266  response1.content['openconfig-network-instance:loc-rib']['routes'] = route
267  d.update(response1.content)
268  show_cli_output("show_ip_bgp_routes.j2", d)
269 
270  elif route_option == "routes":
271  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/global', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER,name1=NAME1)
272  response = api.get(keypath)
273  if(response.ok() and response.content is not None):
274  d.update(response.content)
275  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/rib/afi-safis/afi-safi={afi_safi_name}/{type_name}/neighbors/neighbor={nbr_address}/adj-rib-in-post', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER, name1=NAME1, afi_safi_name=afisafi, type_name=rib_type, nbr_address = neighbour_ip)
276  response1 = api.get(keypath)
277  if(response1.ok() and response1.content is not None):
278  if 'openconfig-network-instance:adj-rib-in-post' in response1.content:
279  route = response1.content['openconfig-network-instance:adj-rib-in-post']['routes']
280  tup = route['route']
281  route['route'] = sorted(tup, key=getPrefix)
282  response1.content['openconfig-network-instance:adj-rib-in-post']['routes'] = route
283  d.update(response1.content)
284  show_cli_output("show_ip_bgp_routes.j2", d)
285  elif route_option == "received-routes":
286  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/global', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER,name1=NAME1)
287  response = api.get(keypath)
288  if(response.ok() and response.content is not None):
289  d.update(response.content)
290  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/rib/afi-safis/afi-safi={afi_safi_name}/{type_name}/neighbors/neighbor={nbr_address}/adj-rib-in-pre', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER, name1=NAME1, afi_safi_name=afisafi, type_name=rib_type, nbr_address = neighbour_ip)
291  response1 = api.get(keypath)
292  if(response1.ok() and response1.content is not None):
293  if 'openconfig-network-instance:adj-rib-in-pre' in response1.content:
294  route = response1.content['openconfig-network-instance:adj-rib-in-pre']['routes']
295  tup = route['route']
296  route['route'] = sorted(tup, key=getPrefix)
297  response1.content['openconfig-network-instance:adj-rib-in-pre']['routes'] = route
298  d.update(response1.content)
299  show_cli_output("show_ip_bgp_routes.j2", d)
300 
301  elif route_option == "advertised-routes":
302  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/global', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER,name1=NAME1)

304  if(response.ok() and response.content is not None):
305  d.update(response.content)

321 def generate_show_bgp_neighbors(args):
322  api = cc.ApiClient()
323  body = None
324  afisafi = "IPV4_UNICAST"
325  vrf = "default"
326  querytype = None
327  i = 0
328  for arg in args:
329  if "vrf" == arg:
330  vrf = args[i+1]
331  elif "ipv4" == arg:
332  afisafi = "IPV4_UNICAST"
333  elif "ipv6" == arg:
334  afisafi = "IPV6_UNICAST"
335  elif "l2vpn" == arg:
336  afisafi = "L2VPN_EVPN"
337  elif "summary" == arg:
338  querytype = 'SUMMARY'
339  i = i + 1
340  d = {}
341  # RPC to fetch the data
342  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/operations/sonic-bgp-show:show-bgp')
343  inputs = {"vrf-name":vrf, "address-family":afisafi}
344  if querytype:
345  inputs['query-type'] = querytype
346 
347  body = {"sonic-bgp-show:input": inputs}
348  response = api.post(keypath, body)
349  if not response:
350  # unknown error (bad input?)
351  return 1
352  if(response.ok()):
353  d = response.content['sonic-bgp-show:output']['response']
354  if len(d) != 0 and "warning" not in d and "Unknown command:" not in d:
355  try:
356  d = json.loads(d, object_pairs_hook=OrderedDict)
357  except:
358  # unknown or missing output
359  return 1
360 
361  if querytype == "SUMMARY":
362  if (not len(d)):
363  print("% No BGP neighbors found")
364  return 1
365  d['max_nbr_col_len'] = len(max(d['peers'].keys(), key=len))
366  d['addr_family'] = afisafi
367  show_cli_output('show_ip_bgp_summary_rpc.j2', d)
368  return 0
369  else:
370  d = json.loads(d)
371  print(d['warning'])
372  else:
373  print response.error_message()
374  return 1

376 def generate_show_bgp_vrf_all(args):
377  api = cc.ApiClient()
378  keypath = []
379  body = None
380 
381  # Use SONIC model to get all configued VRF names
382  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/sonic-vrf:sonic-vrf/VRF/VRF_LIST')
383  sonic_vrfs = api.get(keypath)
384  if sonic_vrfs.ok() and sonic_vrfs.content is not None:
385  args[5] = 'default'
386  d = generate_show_bgp_routes(args)
387  # then show bgp routes on remaining VRF
388  if 'sonic-vrf:VRF_LIST' in sonic_vrfs.content:
389  vrf_list = sonic_vrfs.content['sonic-vrf:VRF_LIST']
390  for vrf in vrf_list:
391  vrf_name = vrf['vrf_name']
392  if vrf_name != 'default':
393  args[5] = vrf_name
394  d = generate_show_bgp_routes(args)

396 def generate_show_bgp_prefix_routes(args):
397  api = cc.ApiClient()
398  keypath = []
399  body = None
400  afisafi = "IPV4_UNICAST"
401  rib_type = "ipv4-unicast"
402  vrf = "default"
403  rfilter = None
404  i = 0
405  for arg in args:
406  if "vrf" == arg:
407  vrf = args[i+1]
408  elif "ipv4" == arg:
409  afisafi = "IPV4_UNICAST"
410  rib_type = "ipv4-unicast"
411  elif "ipv6" == arg:
412  afisafi = "IPV6_UNICAST"
413  rib_type = "ipv6-unicast"
414  elif "prefix" == arg:
415  prefix_ip = args[i+1]
416  elif "bestpath" == arg:
417  rfilter = arg
418  elif "multipath" == arg:
419  rfilter = arg
420  else:
421  if i > 0 and args[0] == 'ip-prefix':
422  prefix_ip = arg
423  else:
424  pass
425  i = i + 1
426  d = { 'vrf': vrf }
427  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/global/config', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER,name1=NAME1)
428  response = api.get(keypath)
429  if(response.ok() and response.content is not None):
430  d.update(response.content)
431  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/rib/afi-safis/afi-safi={afi_safi_name}/{type_name}/openconfig-rib-bgp-ext:loc-rib-prefix/routes/route={prefix_name}', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER, name1=NAME1, afi_safi_name=afisafi, type_name=rib_type, prefix_name=prefix_ip)
432  response1 = api.get(keypath)
433  if(response1.ok() and response1.content is not None):
434  if 'openconfig-rib-bgp-ext:route' in response1.content:
435  if "bestpath" == rfilter:
436  rtList = response1.content['openconfig-rib-bgp-ext:route']
437  for rt in rtList:
438  prfpaths = rt.get('loc-rib-prefix-paths')
439  pathCnt = 0
440  if prfpaths:
441  paths = prfpaths.get('paths')
442  if paths:
443  pathList = paths.get('path')
444  pathCnt = len(pathList)
445  if pathList and pathCnt > 1:
446  bestList = []
447  for path in pathList:
448  state = path.get('state')
449  if state:
450  if state.get('best-path') == True:
451  bestList.append(path)
452  if pathCnt > len(bestList):
453  paths['path'] = bestList
454  pathCnt = len(paths['path'])
455  if pathCnt == 0:
456  del rt['loc-rib-prefix-paths']
457 
458  d.update(response1.content)
459  show_cli_output("show_ip_bgp_prefix_routes.j2", d)
460  return d

462 def generate_show_bgp_peer_groups(args, show_all=False):
463  api = cc.ApiClient()
464  keypath = []
465  body = None
466  pg = None
467  vrf = "default"
468  i = 0
469  for arg in args:
470  if "vrf" == arg:
471  vrf = args[i+1]
472  elif "peer-group" == arg and show_all is False:
473  pg = args[i+1]
474  else:
475  pass
476  i = i + 1
477 
478  d = {}
479 
480  if pg is None:
481  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/peer-groups', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER,name1=NAME1)
482  else:
483  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/peer-groups/peer-group={pgname}', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER,name1=NAME1,pgname=pg)
484  response = api.get(keypath)
485  if(response.ok() and response.content is not None):
486  d.update(response.content)
487  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/global/dynamic-neighbor-prefixes', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER, name1=NAME1)
488  response1 = api.get(keypath)
489  if(response1.ok() and response1.content is not None):
490  d.update(response1.content)
491  show_cli_output("show_bgp_peer_group.j2", d)
492 
493  return d

495 def generate_show_bgp_stats(args):
496  api = cc.ApiClient()
497  keypath = []
498  body = None
499  afisafi = "IPV4_UNICAST"
500  rib_type = "ipv4-unicast"
501  vrf = "default"
502  rfilter = None
503  i = 0
504  for arg in args:
505  if "vrf" == arg:
506  vrf = args[i+1]
507  elif "ipv4" == arg:
508  afisafi = "IPV4_UNICAST"
509  rib_type = "ipv4-unicast"
510  elif "ipv6" == arg:
511  afisafi = "IPV6_UNICAST"
512  rib_type = "ipv6-unicast"
513  else:
514  pass
515  i = i + 1
516  d = { 'vrf': vrf }
517  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/data/openconfig-network-instance:network-instances/network-instance={name}/protocols/protocol={identifier},{name1}/bgp/global/config', name=vrf, identifier=IDENTIFIER,name1=NAME1)
518  response = api.get(keypath)
519  if(response.ok() and response.content is not None):
520  keypath = cc.Path('/restconf/operations/sonic-bgp-show:show-bgp-statistics')
521  body = {"sonic-bgp-show:input": {"vrf-name":vrf, "address-family":afisafi}}
522  response = api.post(keypath, body)
523  if not response:
524  # unknown error (bad input?)
525  return 1
526  if(response.ok()):
527  d = response.content['sonic-bgp-show:output']['response']
528  if len(d) != 0 and "warning" not in d:
529  try:
530  d = json.loads(d)
531  except:
532  # unknown or missing output
533  return 1
534 
535  show_cli_output("show_bgp_stats_rpc.j2", d)

1881 def seconds_to_wdhm_str(seconds):
1882  d = datetime.now()
1883  d = d - timedelta(seconds=int(seconds))
1884  weeks = 0
1885  days = d.day
1886  if days != 0:
1887  days = days - 1
1888  if days != 0:
1889  weeks = days // 7
1890  days = days % 7
1891  if weeks != 0:
1892  wdhm = '{}w{}d{:02}h'.format(int(weeks), int(days), int(d.hour))
1893  elif days != 0:
1894  wdhm = '{}d{:02}h{:02}m'.format(int(days), int(d.hour), int(d.minute))
1895  else:
1896  wdhm = '{:02}:{:02}:{:02}'.format(int(d.hour), int(d.minute), int(d.second))
1897 
1898  return wdhm
1899 
1900 def seconds_to_dhms_str(seconds):
1901  sec = int(seconds)
1902  hours = int(sec)/(60*60)
1903  sec %= (60*60)
1904  minutes = sec/60
1905  sec %= 60
1906  return "%02i:%02i:%02i" % (hours, minutes, sec)
1907 
1908 def get_bgp_nbr_iptype(nbr, afisafiname):
1909  unnumbered = False
1910  is_afmatch = False
1911  nbr_afisafiname = "openconfig-bgp-types:IPV4_UNICAST"
1912  if 'afi-safis' in nbr:
1913  afisafis = nbr['afi-safis']['afi-safi']
1914  for afisafi in afisafis:
1915  if 'state' in afisafi:
1916  nbr_afisafiname = afisafi['state']['afi-safi-name']
1917  else:
1918  nbr_afisafiname = "openconfig-bgp-types:IPV4_UNICAST"
1919  if nbr_afisafiname == afisafiname or afisafiname == 'ipAll':
1920  break
1921  try:
1922  ipaddr = netaddr.IPAddress(nbr['neighbor-address'])
1923  except:
1924  unnumbered = True
1925  if nbr_afisafiname == afisafiname or afisafiname == 'ipAll':
1926  is_afmatch = True
1927  return is_afmatch, unnumbered
1928 
1929 def preprocess_bgp_nbrs(afisafiname, nbrs):
1930  new_nbrs = []
1931  un_enbrs = []
1932  un_pnbrs = []
1933  un_vnbrs = []
1934  un_lnbrs = []
1935  un_nbrs = []
1936  for nbr in nbrs:
1937  is_afmatch = False
1938  unnumbered = False
1939  is_afmatch, unnumbered = get_bgp_nbr_iptype(nbr, afisafiname)
1940 
1941  if is_afmatch:
1942  if 'state' in nbr:
1943  if 'session-state' in nbr['state'] and 'last-established' in nbr['state']:
1944  if nbr['state']['session-state'] == 'ESTABLISHED':
1945  last_estbd = nbr['state']['last-established']
1946  nbr['state']['last-established'] = seconds_to_wdhm_str(last_estbd)
1947  else:
1948  nbr['state']['last-established'] = 'never'
1949 
1950  if 'openconfig-bgp-ext:last-write' in nbr['state']:
1951  last_write = nbr['state']['openconfig-bgp-ext:last-write']
1952  nbr['state']['openconfig-bgp-ext:last-write'] = seconds_to_dhms_str(last_write)
1953 
1954  if 'openconfig-bgp-ext:last-read' in nbr['state']:
1955  last_read = nbr['state']['openconfig-bgp-ext:last-read']
1956  nbr['state']['openconfig-bgp-ext:last-read'] = seconds_to_dhms_str(last_read)
1957 
1958  if 'openconfig-bgp-ext:last-reset-time' in nbr['state']:
1959  last_reset_time = nbr['state']['openconfig-bgp-ext:last-reset-time']
1960  nbr['state']['openconfig-bgp-ext:last-reset-time'] = seconds_to_dhms_str(last_reset_time)
1961 
1962  if unnumbered == True:
1963  ifName = nbr['neighbor-address']
1964  if ifName.startswith("Ethernet"):
1965  un_enbrs.append(nbr)
1966  elif ifName.startswith("PortChannel"):
1967  un_pnbrs.append(nbr)
1968  elif ifName.startswith("Vlan"):
1969  un_vnbrs.append(nbr)
1970  elif ifName.startswith("Loopback"):
1971  un_lnbrs.append(nbr)
1972  else:
1973  un_nbrs.append(nbr)
1974  else:
1975  new_nbrs.append(nbr)
1976 
1977  tup = new_nbrs
1978  new_nbrs = sorted(tup, key=getNbr)
1979  tup = un_enbrs
1980  un_enbrs = sorted(tup, key=getIntfId)
1981  tup = un_pnbrs
1982  un_pnbrs = sorted(tup, key=getIntfId)
1983  tup = un_vnbrs
1984  un_vnbrs = sorted(tup, key=getIntfId)
1985  tup = un_lnbrs
1986  un_lnbrs = sorted(tup, key=getIntfId)
1987  tup = un_nbrs
1988  un_nbr = sorted(tup, key=getIntfId)
1989 
1990  un_enbrs.extend(un_pnbrs)
1991  un_enbrs.extend(un_vnbrs)
1992  un_enbrs.extend(un_lnbrs)
1993  un_enbrs.extend(un_nbrs)
1994  un_enbrs.extend(new_nbrs)
1995  return un_enbrs
1996

2154 def mkArgs2dict(args):
2155  dct = {}
2156  for e in args:

3041 def parseGloblShow(vrf_name, cmd, args=[]):
3042  try:
3043  pipe_idx = args.index('\|')
3044  args = args[:pipe_idx]
3045  except:
3046  # no pipe
3047  pass
3048 
3049  if cmd == 'show bgp l2vpn evpn summary':
3050  return generate_show_bgp_neighbors(args)
3051 
3052  if cmd == 'show bgp ipv4' or cmd == 'show bgp ipv6':
3053  if vrf_name == 'all':
3054  generate_show_bgp_vrf_all(args)
3055  return 0
3056 
3057  if len(args) == 0:
3058  return get_show_bgp(args)
3059  if args[0] == 'statistics':
3060  return generate_show_bgp_stats(args)
3061  elif args[0] == 'ip-prefix':
3062  return generate_show_bgp_prefix_routes(args)
3063  elif args[0] == 'neighbors':
3064  nbr_subcmds = [ 'routes', 'received-routes', 'advertised-routes' ]
3065  if args[-1] in nbr_subcmds:
3066  return generate_show_bgp_routes(args)
3067  elif args[1] == 'neighbor-ip':
3068  response = invoke_show_api('get_ip_bgp_neighbors_neighborip', [ None, vrf_name, 'ipv6' if cmd == 'show bgp ipv6' else 'ipv4', args[-1] ])
3069  show_cli_output('show_ip_bgp_neighbors.j2', response)
3070  elif args[1] == 'interface':
3071  response = invoke_show_api('get_ip_bgp_neighbors_neighborip', [ None, vrf_name, 'ipv6' if cmd == 'show bgp ipv6' else 'ipv4', args[-1] ])
3072  show_cli_output('show_ip_bgp_neighbors.j2', response)
3073  else:
3074  response = invoke_show_api('get_ip_bgp_neighbors', [ None, vrf_name, 'ipv6' if cmd == 'show bgp ipv6' else 'ipv4' ] + args[4:])
3075  show_cli_output('show_ip_bgp_neighbors.j2', response)
3076  return 0
3077  elif args[0] == 'summary':
3078  return generate_show_bgp_neighbors(args)
3079  elif args[0] == 'dampening':

3106 def invoke_parse(pycmd, args=[]):
3107  op = pycmd.split(':')[1]
3108  idx = 1 if op[0] == 'G' else 2
3109  start = idx
3110  end = len(args)
3111  while idx < end:
3112  if args[idx] == '\n':
3113  end = idx
3114  idx += 1
3115  break
3116  elif args[idx][-1] == '\n':
3117  args[idx] = args[idx][:-1]
3118  idx += 1
3119  end = idx
3120  break
3121  idx += 1
3122  cmd = ' '.join(args[start:end])
3123 
3124  if op == 'Gbl':
3125  return parseGlobl(args[0], cmd, args[idx:])
3126  elif op == 'GblV4':
3127  return parseGloblV4(args[0], cmd, args[idx:])
3128  elif op == 'GblV6':
3129  return parseGloblV6(args[0], cmd, args[idx:])
3130  elif op == 'Nbr':
3131  return parseNeigh(args[0], args[1], cmd, args[idx:])
3132  elif op == 'NbrV4':
3133  return parseNeighV4(args[0], args[1], cmd, args[idx:])
3134  elif op == 'NbrV6':
3135  return parseNeighV6(args[0], args[1], cmd, args[idx:])
3136  elif op == 'NbrEvpn':
3137  return parseNeighEvpn(args[0], args[1], cmd, args[idx:])
3138  elif op == 'Pgp':
3139  return parsePeerg(args[0], args[1], cmd, args[idx:])
3140  elif op == 'PgpV4':
3141  return parsePeergV4(args[0], args[1], cmd, args[idx:])
3142  elif op == 'PgpV6':
3143  return parsePeergV6(args[0], args[1], cmd, args[idx:])
3144  elif op == 'PgpEvpn':
3145  return parsePeergEvpn(args[0], args[1], cmd, args[idx:])
3146  elif op == 'GblShow':
3147  return parseGloblShow(args[0], cmd, args[idx:])
3148 
3149  print cc.ApiClient().cli_not_implemented(cmd).error_message()
3150  return 1

3152 def run(func, args):
3153  if func == 'get_show_bgp':
3154  response = invoke_show_api(func, args)
3155  elif func == 'get_ip_bgp_summary':
3156  response = invoke_show_api(func, args)
3157  show_cli_output(args[0], response)
3158  elif func == 'get_ip_bgp_neighbors_neighborip':
3159  response = invoke_show_api(func, args)
3160  show_cli_output(args[0], response)
3161  elif func == 'get_ip_bgp_neighbors':
3162  response = invoke_show_api(func, args)
3163  show_cli_output(args[0], response)
3164  elif func == 'get_show_bgp_prefix':
3165  response = invoke_show_api(func, args)
3166  elif func == 'get_show_bgp_peer_group':
3167  response = invoke_show_api(func, args)
3168  elif func == 'get_show_bgp_peer_group_all':
3169  response = invoke_show_api(func, args)
3170  elif func[:9] == '_PyParse:':
3171  ret = invoke_parse(func, args)
3172  if ret != 0:
3173  return 1
3174  else:
3175  response = invoke_api(func, args)
3176  if response.ok():
3177  if response.content is not None:
3178  # Get Command Output
3179  api_response = response.content
3180  print(api_response)
3181  if api_response is None:
3182  print("Failed")
3183  return 1
3184  else:
3185  print response.error_message()
3186  return 1
